< text>
They have great selections of fresh and salt water fishes, and pet birds from time to time. Pet supplies on the wall was a little bit tricky to find because it look a bit messy at first, but it gets better as time goes by and by the time you are less disoriented and learnt their logic of placing stuffs around. Although it's a small pet store, but you will be able to get what you want. Decent price. Easy to find parking on the streets and the owner couples speak Spanish, English and Chinese< /text>

< text>
I'm a second generation customer of this pet store. They have been our go to store for about 20 years. Joe is very knowledgeable (& bilingual!) about the animals. I go to his store for everything I need for my parrot I was gifted from his store 17 years ago. Family run and family owned. I don't know what I'd do without them.< /text>

< Review>
If I can give this place 10 stars I will... I will because Joe and Doris (owner) there really nice person always with a smile on there face always there to help you. They have anything you need from salt water fish, fresh water, birds and dogs, cats, hamsters, snakes any kind of animal you might have at home. Whatever you need believe me you will find it here and if you dont see it just ask him he will get it for you. I come here because I have a salt water tank at home with his advice he guide on what to do what I need with my tank and so far is been 2 years none of my fish have die.
But I just gotta say come check it out there really nice people there prices on everything are good/fair I'm just so lucky to have them close to my house in my city.
Thank you Joe and Doris for everything you guys do and treat everyone keep up the good work.</Review>

< Review>
Awesome place for a walk, bike, or horse ride. You can take a short one mile walk around the lake area or it connects with the entire Rohr Park area. The trails are wide with plenty of space. Reviews are very nice especially right now with all the flowers blooming. Easy to get to and plenty of parking. There are even picnic spots available and benches to sit and look at the lake.< /Review>

<date>1570072177878< /date><rate>5</rate>< Review>
Awesome location with so much to offer. Right in the heart of Bonita and there is so much to do here with endless opportunity to hike, mountain bike and even ride a horse. You can go all the way to San Diego Bay from here or up go inland to San Miguel mountain but riding a horse you're limited to Bonita up to San Miguel mountain. The lake is beautiful and takes about 15-20 min to walk around and it's one of my favorite places to do photo shoots here in the South Bay.< /Review>

There have been few times in my life where I have been taken back when meeting a service provider. This is one of those cases.

When Omar showed up he was on the phone with the home warranty company that I use speaking about my issue, the one I relayed to the company, before his arrival.

He told me all was going to be okay, but my garage spring is one that needs to be ordered due to it being custom. I understood.

The thing that stood out was his inquiries as to how the doors are acting, what they are doing and what they aren't doing. He was not up-selling me anything and he was direct and to the point.

There was no romance in the way in which he was presenting, it was just the facts with a constant reassurement the job will be done correctly when the spring arrives and he returns.

I'm glad to have met Omar from Safeway Garage Doors. The clincher, I have had other garage techs out here who wanted to sell me garage doors in a different configuration than I have. All to the cost of thousands of dollars. When I asked Omar, he said I have the best configuration and there is nothing wrong with the garage doors I have. They are in great shape.

Refreshing for sure.< /text>< pics>

I have been a major fan of this place for years!  Today's visit was no different.  I appreciated their COVID-19 precaution: table spacing, outdoor seating option, plexiglass barriers between booths, sealed condiments, etc.  As always, the food was on point and super quick.  Friendly staff and good service have always been a staple.  I would recommend this place for anyone wanting some great Mexican Food!  I would also suggest that you try the soups - they're great.  Also, try the "Mexican Parrillada" if you are with someone that you don't mind eating off the same plate as.</Review>

<Time>1563214376456< /Time><rating>2</rating>< review>
I haven't been to this place in many, many years. I moved 4 years ago, but was back in Cali visiting my mom, son, daughter in law, and friends. The prices have sky rocketed $15-20  per dish. You get one small basket of chips for 4 people, and the chips at the bottom were all broken. If you want more chips it's $2.00 extra. It didn't matter if you are eating alone or with 4 people the basket of chips was the same size. Black beans $1.00 extra. They said they use the same size shrimp for all dishes. We got 3 different dishes of shrimp and they were all different sizes the shrimp. You ask the waitress and she says I am just following the rules. The service was so slow. You had to ask for refills. The food was ok not the best. There are so many other Mexican restaurant that is better food, and doesn't care if you want another basket of chips. The total bill for 4 people was over $80.00. My mom talked to the manager when we left because as we were walking out this table had one person sitting there and there chips was piled high for one. <text>Came here on a Thursday for lunch. It's an institution in ENCINITAS I suppose, been here since 1977, so I had higher expectations. Fairly decent crowd so many must like it. I was underwhelmed.
From the start, the salsa was average at best, probably not homemade, really basic, not spicy and too tomatoe-y, but salsa is never ever that bad, so I digress.
The carne asada burrito combo was not great. Every bit of vegetable, peppers, onions and especially the lettuce looked days old and very wilted. The lettuce was frankly pretty close to brown as was the avocado.
Then on the side is a scoop of, I guess,  some sort of slaw. Again, pretty wilty looking.
I was quite surprised I had to ask for some hot sauce, tapatio, cholula, etc. None of any sort on any of the tables.
Service was fairly prompt and courteous. Price is reasonable if only a little fresher ingredients.< /text></record>

<user_name>spudhufer</user_name>< date>
1407953066678<//date>

< review>
La Especial Norte has been around forever and has always had a reputation for featuring some traditional dishes not commonly found on most Mexican restaurant menus.
I learned the hard way that most of these dishes like the Molcajete, strips of beef or chicken, baby cactus a special sauce on sizzling hot stone bowl, are not on the lunch menu.
I still had a nice lunch.

What I ate....

Shrimp Cocktail ~ Shrimp, avocado, hot sauce, cucumber, onion, cilantro

This is one of my favorite dished and I always order one if a restaurant offers it. Their version was good with a balance of all the ingredients.

Chicken Soup ~ Shredded chicken, avocado, tomato, rice, cilantro

Note ~ The stock had a lot of depth of flavor.

Chicken Mole ~ Shredded chicken, mole, rice, and beans.

Note ~ Good mole is hard to find, when done right it almost has a spicy earthiness to it. Their mole is very good.

I will have to go back for dinner to try the larger menu, still the lunch deals are very good ~ Entree w / rice and beans, Drink, Cup of chicken soup, and cabbage salad for $8.50< /review>

< Review>
This is a wonderful Mexican restaurant located on the "original" coast highway in the northernmost part of Encinitas, actually closer to being in Leucadia. The food is very good, although I have had equally good Mexican dishes elsewhere. The service is very friendly and fast. The parking lot is VERY limited in size to you may have a bit of trouble with that.

They have a dish that I really, really love and that is hard to find elsewhere: Milanesas. This is where they bread and fry a tenderized piece of flank steak or chicken breast and serve it with salsa and chopped cilantro over it. THAT is a great entree! For even more milanesa goodness, ask them to cover it with enchilada sauce and grated cheese. Muy sabroso!</Review>
